< text>
Happy Hour menu items were delicious and reasonably priced. It was my 1st time there, as I was recommended to come here by a friend.

The service, however, our Server's name was Amy. She had an accent, definitely not from here. And not sure if she was new. In our party of 5, most of us had debit/credit cards. So we requested to split checks by 3. I paid cash. She said there was an automatic charge for gratuity for 5 or more people in a table. I didn't see that information anywhere in the website. After mixing up the orders on the different receipts, and mixing up the payment options on the receipts, we told her that the orders were wrong on the receipts. Even though it was almost the same price on the receipts, she blurted out: "It doesn't matter!" She was rude and took a long time getting the corrected receipts back to us. She should not be in a customer service job if she can't handle a little stress without being rude to her customers.  I'm not coming here again. We were so annoyed by her as we walked back to our cars. That was a bad 1st impression for me for Los Locos.<//text>

I like how simple this place is.
If you‚Äôre coming here it‚Äôs because this is what you like and you want it.
No confusion. Great for indecisive people lol

The Menu is short and easy:
- Fried chicken Sliders
Spice levels:
Mild / Hot / Extra Hot
- Grilled corn
- Mac N cheese
- Fries / Cheese Fries

I tried the Mild and Hot sliders.
The slaw was fantastic. The chicken was really good. The buns could be a little softer but they are still good. I just like Hawaiian bread more than usual.
You can get extra sauce to dip in. Some honey on the side to make it sweet n spicy if you like.
Good sized portions so guaranteed to get u full.
The grilled corn was OUTTA HERE. Great flavor with a bit of butter and garlic and some char from the grill. It was a full on corn on the Cob instead of just a piece of one.
I do recommend you come by this place and try it.

Cool chill vibe. Nice music playlist. Dog friendly and outdoor seating and benches.< /review>

<date>1556322061273<//date><pics>None<//pics>< Text>
This is such a unique experience. The chicken sliders (2 for $12) -- that chicken is to die for. If you do NOT like spicy (as in HOT), order the mild or less. The "Hot" is genuinely hot, and I like hot things like habanero and serrano, jalapeno, etc. I ordered the hot version and I'm glad I didn't opt for the extra-hot or I don't think I could have done it. The fries are super crisp and moist. And even though they are the only thing not scratch-made, the churros were the very best I've ever, ever, ever had. I understand they get them from a local bakery. I may need to camp out to see if that bakery is identified in a delivery van or something.... Anyway, this place is open LATE and it's off the beaten path (which is so nice) so it's a bit more "local" - like, but just amazing food here. Service with a smile, fast, friendly, hot, fresh....what's not to love. Go here.< /Text>

<Name>Gevork Asatryan< /Name><time>1538258412896<//time><rating>3<//rating>< Text>
Here's my thought about this joint. They have long since been on my list of places to try out and I finally visit them last week right around 7pm on a Friday (hour after they opened up). I ordered two chicken sliders and their specialty "secret" fries thats topped off with Mac n Cheese and fried chicken. The sign said "30 mins from here on out" after I placed my order.

1. The seating area was scarce and the amount of customers had over filled the area.

2. I waited over an hour to get some fried chicken. I mean cmon! 75 minute to get some chicken sliders that I paid $30 for seems insane. After I placed my order I overheard someone say they've been waiting for 50 minutes already. The least they could have done is changed that sign to something more reasonable especially when the first customers that had arrived waited double that.

3. I ordered some corn on the cobs in the meantime because I was starving and just FYI - the hot cheetos corn is no longer available there. Prepare for $3 corns that are skinny as a stick with hardly any meat on the bones.

4. If you're not into really spicy stuff make sure you choose mild spice! The hot seemed extreme to us. Don't even want to know what the extra hot tastes like.

As far as food quality goes, it was really nothing special. It was more of a hype than anything. You can tell their ingredients were mediocre and they had boxes of food sitting on the floor outside in the back probably due to lack of storage space. Ya definitely not worth the hour wait. $6 for a chicken slider... Just order elsewhere and you'd be more satisfied.< /Text>

<UserId.>116849946697029256338<//UserId.><rating>5< /rating><Response>None<//Response><Time>1533766624505< /Time>< Review>
I was craving some fried chicken and decided to give this place a try.
From the outside it looks like a really cool food truck that‚Äôs been installed inside of a building, in a tiny parking lot. But once you go inside you see how alive this place is. From the really cool art work on the wall and the mosaic style chairs it has a very young and fun vibe to it.
I love how the menu is hand written and as I peaked through the ordering window I noticed how all the chefs were singing and dancing and just enjoying making the food. A very nice gentleman approached us and started to recommend some popular / must-have items: the chicken sliders, and corn and cheese fries. So of course we said yes, yes and yes PLEASE! We finished our order and sat down and not long after everything came out together, which if you know me you know I love ! If it‚Äôs not appetizers it all should come out together. And Trap knows that very well! As I picked up one of the sliders I could just see the juiciness of it and all the delicious ingredients. I bit into it and it was heaven! The chicken was so tender yet the outside was so crispy. It was spicy but mild. The cold slaw that was bedded under it was amazingly fresh and citrusy. And the bun was very fluffy. It was the best fried chicken slider! Next: the corn on the cob. I don‚Äôt know what they glaze this corn with but they should keep doing it. It was very buttery and soft. As I was biting into it the corn would fall off of the cob. Fantastic! Last but not least, the cheese fries! OH MY GOF - hold the press!! Where did this come from? How did they manage to make the fries crispy AND soft at the same time?! And the cheese and sauce on top was the perfect addition to the already perfect fries. Later on I found out that they make their own sauces and dressing in house - which made me enjoy the food that much more. Let‚Äôs just put it this way, I loved everything so much that I didn‚Äôt let a single fry go to waste, I got whatever that was left all to go AND ordered 4 more corn on the cob to go. Yes, 4! Don‚Äôt judge me lol
To say my experience and the food at Trap Fried Chicken was fantastic is an understatement. I can not wait to go back and try more delicious food.
Also, they have this amazing watermelon basil drink that is not too sweet and is just delightful to have!<//Review>

< review>
Mmm, there‚Äôs really no substitution for a good bagel, and Posh Bagel is pretty darn good. ü•Ø The best bagel I‚Äôve ever had? No. But better than most other places in the area!

The shop has a nice vibe, consistent with its name, and is well lit and clean.

They have a good assortment of bagels; all the usual suspects you‚Äôd want to see at a bagel joint, as well as some more exotic options if you feel like living on the edge.

They also have a huge assortment of options for you to customize your order. Sinatra would love this place cause they let you do it Your Way.

While I didn‚Äôt try any of their cafe drinks, they seemed to have all the expected options, plus if you don‚Äôt want a coffee/cafe drink, they have what appeared to be just about every bottled drink you could want to choose from.

The employees didn‚Äôt seem enthusiastic or friendly toward the customers, but they were efficient and had my order ready very quickly. My only comment would be that my bagel could hav been toasted slightly more, but I‚Äôll assume that was my fault for not asking for it well toasted.</review>

< review>
From the various bagel places I've tried in the surrounding area, this is probably the best. Almost on par with New York City bagels. I tried Noah's bagel near by and it just doesn't compare. For some reason, the Noah's bagel here is much different than the Noah's Bagel in NYC. The Noah's Bagel in NYC is one of my favorites, along with NYC Bagel & Coffee House.

I do believe that the spread options at Noah's bagel is better compared to here but this place gives you just the right amount of spread. I think Noah's gives you a little less.  The spreads are fresh and they don't skimp out on the ingredients. For example, if you're getting honey walnut spread, you'll get more than one walnut per bite.

If you ask for half the bagel with one spread and another half of the bagel with a different spread, depending on the worker, you will get both spreads on the same half when cut. It shouldn't be like this but I can see how easily this could happen.  Another great thing about this place is they have quite a few options for mini bagels. Great option for kids.

I think the coffee here is better than the one at Noah's. The service here is excellent. There's always a line when I come here in the morning so try to come early, especially with covid restrictions.

Overall I would highly recommend this place and will come back again!<//review>

I've been a customer of Bell Pest Control for many years to deal with ants and mice, and they've been very responsive. Recently there has been a real problem in Elk Grove with cockroaches that infiltrate homes from the sewers. I found several in my garage and called Bell for an additional service. It was almost time for my bimonthly service so the call center moved it up to the next day. I got a call from the technician, Matt, the evening I called and we arranged a more specific time for his visit, which was really helpful. When he arrived I described the problems with the sewer roaches and we had an interesting conversation about bugs. Matt sprayed around the property. <response>{'time': 1615483208141, 'text': 'Alicia, thank you for being a client and for taking the time to write a review about your service and your technician. We appreciate your business - Bell Pest Control'}</response>< Text>
I have had Bell Pest Control Service since I purchased my first home in 2014. I recently purchased a new home in February and within the first month I had a large ant infestation in my home after an ant nest was disturbed following yard work that was done before I purchased the home. I haven't had to do any work in the yard yet, so it wasn't me:-) I called the office first thing in the morning hoping someone could come that day before the ants made it into my pantry. I wish I could remember the name of who I spoke with. She was absolutely lovely, sympathetic and went above and beyond to get techs to my house that afternoon. If I recall, she mentioned that she lives in Galt, I hope that helps her supervisor identify her.
Osmand and Isiah arrived that afternoon to spray inside and out, inspected my attic to make sure there were no rodents (as the home inspection noted some old droppings up there) and they inspected the backyard to see where the ants were coming from. Sure enough, Isiah was able to identify the source and followed the ant trail clear across my backyard to my fruit trees. They treated the area and walked me through everything they did before leaving. We set up a follow-up appointment for Osmand to return two-weeks later to check on the bait he placed in the attic and check on the ant situation.
At our follow-up appointment I informed Osmand that I thought there may be a dead rodent in my wall and I had been smelling it since the day I moved in, he also smelt it. He went straight to the attic, checked the old bait and placed an odor absorption bag in my attic to help with the odor as he couldn't find the animal. OMG it has only been an hour and the smell is already improving. He treated the backyard again as there was still a decent ant trail moving along my patio, but luckily no more ants in the house!! WOOHOO
In my opinion, Bell Pest Control is great. I have always lucked out getting truly amazing techs that seem to go above and beyond. They are always so professional, personable and genuine.
Thank You
Alicia</Text>

Extremely disappointed with our experience in discontinuing our services with Bell Pest Control due to moving out of the property. We are CONTINUING to be charged for services at that property despite following all the proper channels, i.e. written notification requesting cancellation of service, verbal notification on NUMEROUS occasions AND notifying our service person, Steve (who was always great, btw...too bad they don't hire his degree of honesty & integrity in the office), that we had cancelled the services. We ultimately had to file a fraudulant charge claim with our bank against Bell Pest Control in order to rectify the situation, get the charges reversed and prevent them from posting additional charges to our account. **We were treated extremely rudely by their staff members and were basically told "too bad" when they were unable to 'find' our paperwork.

Think twice before using them...do you want to be charged for services not rendered and continue to pay for those services even after you've vacated the property? We'll be making a report to the BBB, as well as informing everyone we know of our experience.

It appears, from the other reviews here, that this is a pattern with Bell Pest Control. Do your homework before signing up...shady business practices do not make for happy customers, nor long-term customers!

Todd and Claudia Speelman< /review>
